译者介绍
杨文轩
华中科技大学硕士，擅长Web 2.0开
发，有丰富的对日开发经验，现就职于
日本方正股份有限公司。译作有《图解
Java多线程设计模式》《图解基础设施
设计模式》《C现代编程：集成开发环
境、设计模式、根限编程、测试驱动开
发、重构、持续集成》及《图解设计模
式，

## Page 5

<span style="font-family:'FZHTJW--GB1-0';font-size:10.50pt;color:#181818">内  容  提  要</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">本书是一本</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818"> 代码优化指南。作者精选了他在近</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">30</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818"> 年编程生涯中最频繁使用的技术和</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">能够带来最大性能提升效果的技术，旨在让读者在提升</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818"> 程序的同时，思考优化软件之美。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">书中主要内容有：代码优化的意义和总原则，与优化相关的计算机硬件背景知识，性能分析方</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">法及工具，优化字符串的使用，算法、动态分配内存、热点语句、查找与排序等等的优化方法。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">本书适合所有</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818"> 程序员，也可供其他语言的程序员优化代码时作为参考。</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">著　　　　</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">[</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">美</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">] Kurt Guntheroth</span>

<span style="font-family:'Helvetica-Bold';font-size:26.83pt;font-weight:bold;color:#181818">O’Reilly Media, Inc.</span><span style="font-family:'HYb2gj';font-size:26.83pt;color:#181818">介绍</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818">O’Reilly Media</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818"> 通过图书、杂志、在线服务、调查研究和会议等方式传播创新知识。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818">自</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818">1978</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818"> 年开始，</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818">O’Reilly</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818"> 一直都是前沿发展的见证者和推动者。超级极客们正在开创</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818">着未来，而我们关注真正重要的技术趋势——通过放大那些“细微的信号”来刺激社</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818">会对新科技的应用。作为技术社区中活跃的参与者，</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818">O’Reilly</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818"> 的发展充满了对创新的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818">倡导、创造和发扬光大。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818">O’Reilly</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818"> 为软件开发人员带来革命性的“动物书”；创建第一个商业网站（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818">GNN</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818">）；组</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818">织了影响深远的开放源代码峰会，以至于开源软件运动以此命名；创立了</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Italic';font-size:10.00pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">Make</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818"> 杂志，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818">从而成为</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818">DIY</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818"> 革命的主要先锋；公司一如既往地通过多种形式缔结信息与人的纽带。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818">O’Reilly</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818"> 的会议和峰会集聚了众多超级极客和高瞻远瞩的商业领袖，共同描绘出开创</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818">新产业的革命性思想。作为技术人士获取信息的选择，</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818">O’Reilly</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818"> 现在还将先锋专家的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818">知识传递给普通的计算机用户。无论是通过图书出版、在线服务或者面授课程，每一</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818">项</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818">O’Reilly</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818"> 的产品都反映了公司不可动摇的理念——信息是激发创新的力量。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">业界评论</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZKTJW--GB1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818">“</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818">O</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818">’</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818">Reilly Radar</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTJW--GB1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#181818"> 博客有口皆碑。”</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZKTJW--GB1-0';font-size:11.00pt;color:#181818">但我还是要感谢我的妻子</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:11.00pt;color:#181818">Renee Ostler</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTJW--GB1-0';font-size:11.00pt;color:#181818">，是她让本书得以出版。她为我腾出</span>

## Page 20

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">读者朋友，你好！我的名字叫</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Kurt</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">，是一名狂热的编程爱好者。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">我编写软件已经超过</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">35</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 年了。我从未就职于微软、谷歌、</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Facebook</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">、苹果或者其他知名</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">公司。但是在这些年里，除了几个短暂的假期外，我每天都在写代码。最近</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">20</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 年里，我</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">几乎只编写</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 程序，并与其他睿智的开发人员讨论</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">。所以我有资格写一本关于优</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">化</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 代码的书。我还发表过许多文章，包括规范、评论、手册、学习笔记以及博客文章</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">http://oldhandsblog.blogspot.com</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）等。有时令我吃惊的是，我共事过的睿智能干的程序员</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">中，只有半数能将两个符合英文语法的句子合并在一起。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">我最喜欢的名言之一出自艾萨克</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:7.00pt;color:#181818">•</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 牛顿爵士的一封信。他在信中写道：“我之所以看得更</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">远，是因为我站在巨人的肩上。”现在，我也站在巨人的肩上了，特别是阅读过他们的著</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">作：有优雅的小书，如</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Brian Kernighan</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Dennis Ritchie</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 合著的《</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 程序设计语言》；有</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">充满智慧且走在技术前沿的书籍，如</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Scott Meyers</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">Effective C</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 系列；有充满挑战又能</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">扩展思维的书籍，如</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Andrei Alexandrescu</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的《</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 设计新思维》；有科学严谨且讲解准确</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">的书籍，如</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Bjarne Stroustrup</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Margaret Ellis</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 合著的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">The Annotated C</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">++</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818"> Reference Manual</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">在我职业生涯的大部分时间，我都从没想过有一天可以自己写一本书。但是突然有一天，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">我发现我需要写这本书。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">那么为什么我要写一本关于</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 性能优化的书呢？</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">在</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">21</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 世纪初期，</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 曾一度受到诟病。</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 语言的支持者指出</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 程序的性能不如以</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 语</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">言编写的相同代码。拥有巨额营销预算的著名企业吹嘘它们自己的面向对象语言，宣称</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 语言难以使用，而它们的工具才是未来。各大高校也决定教授</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Java</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 语言，因为它有一</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">套免费的工具链。由于以上种种原因，大公司投资大笔金钱使用</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Java</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">、</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C#</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 或是</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">PHP</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 来编</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">写网站和操作系统。</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 看起来正在逐渐衰落。对于任何相信</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 语言是强大且有用的工</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">具的人而言，那是一段困难的时期。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">就在这时，一件有趣的事情发生了。处理器核心的处理速度停止增长，但是工作负荷在持</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">续加大。于是，那些大公司又开始重新雇用</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 程序员去解决它们的扩容问题。用</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">从头开始重新编写代码的成本变得比在数据中心消耗的电费要便宜。突然之间，</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 再度</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">流行起来了。</span>

## Page 21

<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 与</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">2016</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 年年初那些高市场份额的编程语言</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:5.54pt;color:#181818">1</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">相比非常突出的一点是，它为开发人员提</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">供了一连串的可选实现方式，从全自动、自动支持到精准手动控制。</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 赋予了开发人员</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">掌控性能权衡的力量，这种掌控让性能优化成为可能。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">市面上介绍如何优化</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 代码的书并不多。其中之一是由</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Dov Bulka</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 与</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">David Mayhew</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 精</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">心研究所著，不过现在看来有些过时的《提高</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 性能的编程技术》。这两位作者似乎与</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">我有相似的职业经历，也发现了很多相同的优化原则。若想看看其他人怎么看待本书中提</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">出的问题，推荐从《提高</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 性能的编程技术》开始。另外，</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Scott Meyers</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 等人也广泛地</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">讨论过如何避免使用复制构造函数。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">需要掌握的关于代码优化的知识太多了，足够写出</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 本书。在本书中，我精选出了自己</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">在工作中频繁使用的技术和能够带来最大性能提升效果的技术进行讲解。奋战在性能优化</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">前线的读者可能会有疑问，为什么本书中没有介绍任何有助于他们解决问题的对策。对于</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">这些疑问，我只能说：“对不起，内容太多，篇幅有限。”</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">欢迎大家将勘误、评论和最喜欢的优化策略发送至</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">antelope_book@guntheroth.com</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">我热爱软件开发。我享受永不停歇地练习每一种新的循环方式和接口。</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">编写代码是一门科</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">学，也是一门写诗艺术；它是一项冷僻的技术，一种内在的艺术形式，以至于除了少数同</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">行外几乎没有人懂得欣赏它。优雅的函数中蕴藏着美感，被广泛使用的强大的惯用法中蕴</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">藏着智慧。但令人遗憾的是，每一部史诗般的软件诗篇（如</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Stepanov</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的标准模板库），都</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">对应着</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10 000</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 行单调、庞大、枯燥的代码。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">本书的根本目标是帮助读者思考优化软件之美。请记住这一点并践行之。请看得更远一些！</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">为本书中的代码致歉</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">虽然我已经编写和优化</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 代码超过</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">20</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 年了，但是本书中所出现的大多数代码都是特意</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">为本书编写的。就像所有新编写的代码一样，这些代码也会有缺陷。为此，我深表歉意。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">多年以来，我一直为</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">、</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 和各种嵌入式系统进行开发，而本书中展示的代</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">码则是我在</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 上编写的。因此，毫无疑问，本书中的代码和内容都更加偏向于</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">。那些使用</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 操作系统中的</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Visual Studio</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 讲解的优化</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 代码的技术，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">同样也适用于</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">、</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Mac OS X</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 或者其他</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 环境。不过，不同优化方式的正确使用时</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">机则取决于编译器和标准库的实现以及代码是在哪种处理器上测试的。优化是一门实验科</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">学。盲目地信任优化建议往往会失望。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">我知道在不同的编译器之间、</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Unix</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 系统和嵌入式系统之间存在的兼容性是非常难以应对</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">的。如果书中的代码无法在你最喜爱的系统上编译通过，我感到非常抱歉。本书并不会讲</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">解跨系统的兼容性，我个人倾向于展示简单的代码。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">我并不喜欢下面这种大括号缩进风格：</span>
<span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:8.50pt;color:#181818">if (bool_condition) { </span>
<span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:8.50pt;color:#181818">    controlled_statement(); </span>
<span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:8.50pt;color:#181818">}</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">注</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">1</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">：可以从</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">http://www.tiobe.com/tiobe-index/</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818"> 查询各编程语言的市场份额。——译者注</span>
<span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">xviii   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">｜</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">前言</span>

## Page 22

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">不过，这种风格的优点是可以在一页中放入更多的代码行，因此，我选择在本书中使用这</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">种风格。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">示例代码的使用</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">可从以下地址下载本书示例代码、解决方案示例等附带资料：</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">guntheroth.com</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">本书是要帮你完成工作的，所以书中的示例代码通常可以直接拿去用在你的程序或文档</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">中。除非你使用了很大一部分代码，否则无需联系我们获得许可。比如，用本书的几个</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">代码片段写一个程序就无需获得许可，销售或分发</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">O</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">’</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Reilly</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 图书的示例光盘则需要获得许</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">可；引用本书中的示例代码回答问题无需获得许可，将书中大量的代码放到你的产品文档</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">中则需要获得许可。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">我们很希望但并不强制要求你在引用本书内容时加上引用说明。引用说明一般包括书名、</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">作者、出版社和</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">ISBN</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">，比如“</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Italic';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">Optimized C++</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> by Kurt Guntheroth(O</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">’</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Reilly). Copyright 2016 </span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Kurt Guntheroth, 978-1-491-92206-4</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">”。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">如果你觉得自己对示例代码的用法超出了上述许可的范围，欢迎你通过</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">permissions@</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">oreilly.com</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 与我们联系。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">排版约定</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">本书使用了下列排版约定。</span>

## Page 24

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">这是一个充满了计算的世界。许多程序都需要全天候运行，无论这些代码是运行于手表、</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">手机、平板电脑、工作站、超级计算机上，抑或是数据中心覆盖全球的网络中。所以，仅</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">仅是准确地将你脑海中的很棒的想法转换为代码是不够的；甚至梳理所有代码以找出缺</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">陷，直到程序可以一直正确地运行也是不够的。你的应用程序可能会在客户所能提供的硬</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">件上运行得非常缓慢；你的硬件团队可能会只给你一个微处理器，却要求你满足他们巨大</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">的性能开销目标；你可能正在与竞争对手就吞吐量和帧数战斗着；或者你正在将一个项目</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">推广至全球用户，但有点担心可能会把事情弄砸了。那么，请进入优化的世界。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">这是一本关于优化的书，特别是引用了一些</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 代码特有的行为模式对</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 程序进行优</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">化。书中的一些优化技术也适用于其他编程语言，但是我并不会以一种通用的方式讲解这</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">些技术。有些对</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 代码特别有效的优化技术，可能对其他编程语言没有效果，甚至根</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">本不可行。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">本书关注的是如何对体现</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 设计最佳实践的正确代码进行优化，使之不仅可以体现出优</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">秀的</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 设计，而且还可以在绝大多数计算机上更快速、更低耗地运行。许多优化机会的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">出现源于某些</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 特性被误用而导致程序运行缓慢、消耗许多资源。这些代码虽然是正确</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">的，却不完善。这些代码往往是因为开发人员缺乏现代微处理器设备的基本常识，或是没</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">有仔细考虑各种</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 对象构建方式的性能开销而编写出的。可进行优化的另外一个原因</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">是，</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 提供了对内存管理和复制的精准控制功能。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">本书不会涉及编写汇编语言子程序、计算时钟周期，或者学习英特尔最新的芯片可以同</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">时分发多少个指令。确实有一些开发人员会为某个单一平台（例如</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Xbox</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:5.54pt;color:#181818">1</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 就是一个很好的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">例子）工作数年，他们不仅有充足的时间，而且也需要去掌握在该平台中进行开发的秘</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">注</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">1</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">：</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818"> Xbox</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818"> 是由美国微软公司开发的家用电视游戏机。</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">——</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">译者注</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYe3gj';font-size:19.00pt;color:#181818">第</span><span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:19.00pt;color:#181818">1</span><span style="font-family:'HYe3gj';font-size:19.00pt;color:#181818"> 章</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYb2gj';font-size:26.83pt;color:#181818">优化概述</span>

<span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1</span>

<span style="font-family:'MicrosoftYaHei';font-size:8.00pt;color:#b4b4b4">图灵社区会员 ChenyangGao(2339083510@qq.com) 专享 尊重版权</span>

![](./C++性能优化指南 (甘瑟尔罗斯) (Z-Library)_assets/images/p024_img01.png)

---

## Page 25

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">诀。但是，绝大多数开发人员还是会为手机、平板电脑或</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">PC</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 等含有各种不同微处理器芯</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">片（甚至有些芯片还没有被设计出来）的设备开发程序。那些嵌入式软件的开发人员也必</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">须面对拥有不同体系结构的各种处理器。完全掌握这些处理器的特性只会让开发人员疯狂</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">和犹豫不决。我不建议你选择这条路。对于大多数应用程序来说，对每种处理器都进行特</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">定的优化是难以取得好效果的，因为这些应用程序必须运行于各种处理器之上。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">本书也不会教授如何以最快的独立于操作系统的方式在</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">、</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">、</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">OS X</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 以及所</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">有的嵌入式操作系统上进行操作。本书会告诉你能用</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（包括</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 标准库）做什么。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">脱离了</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 进行优化可能会让他人难以评审或评价优化后的代码。我们不应当轻易采取</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">这种方式。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">本书将讲解如何进行优化。任何不更新的技术或者功能都注定失败，因为新的算法被不断</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">地发明出来，新的编程语言特性也在不断地涌现。而本书则提供了一些可以运行的示例来</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">展示如何逐步地改善代码。通过这个过程，你可以熟悉代码的优化过程并形成一种可以提</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">高优化效果的思维模式。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">本书也会讲解如何优化编码过程。注重程序在运行时的性能开销的开发人员，可以从一开</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">始就编写出高效代码。通过不断地练习，编写高效代码通常并不会比编写低效代码花费更</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">多时间。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">最后，这本书是关于创造奇迹的，是关于在检查性能变化时听见一位同事惊叹：“哇，到</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">底发生了什么？才启动就处理完毕了。有人做了什么修改吗？”优化也是一件可以提升开</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">发人员的地位和自豪感的事情。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">1.1</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">　优化是软件开发的一部分</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">优化是一项编码活动。在传统的软件开发过程中，直到编码完成，项目进入了集成与测试</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">阶段，能够观察到程序整体的性能时，才会进行优化。而在敏捷开发方式中，当一个带有</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">性能指标的特性编码完成后或是需要实现特定的性能目标时，就会分配一个或多个</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">冲刺</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">sprint</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）进行优化。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">性能优化的目的是通过改善正确程序的行为使其满足客户对处理速度、吞吐量、内存占用</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">以及能耗等各种指标的需求。因此，性能优化与编码对开发过程而言有着同等的重要性。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">对于用户而言，性能糟糕得让人无法接受，这个问题的严重程度不亚于出现</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">bug</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 和未实现</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">的特性。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">bug</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 修复与性能优化之间的一个重要区别是，性能是一个连续变量。特性要么是实现了，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">要么是没有实现；</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">bug</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 要么存在，要么不存在。但是性能可以是非常糟糕或者非常优秀，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">还可能是介于这二者之间的某种程度。优化还是一个迭代的过程。每当程序中最慢的部分</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">被改善后，一个新的最慢的部分就会出现。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">与其他编码任务相比，优化更像是一门实验科学，需要有更深入的科学思维方式。要想优</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">化成功，需要先观察程序行为，然后基于这些程序行为作出可测试的推测，再进行实验得</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">出测试结果。这些测试结果要么验证推测，要么推翻推测。经验丰富的开发人员常常相信</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">他们对于最优代码具有足够的经验和直觉。但是除非他们频繁地测试自己的直觉，否则通</span>
<span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">2   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">｜</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">第</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1</span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章</span>

---

## Page 26

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">常他们都是错误的。在我个人为本书编写测试代码的经历中，就多次出现测试结果与我的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">直觉相悖的情况。实验，而非直觉，才是贯穿本书的主题。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">1.2</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">　优化是高效的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">开发人员很难理解单个编码决策对大型程序的整体性能的影响。因此，实际上所有完整的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">程序都包含大量的优化机会。即使是经验丰富的团队在时间充裕的情况下编写出的代码，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">运行速度通常也可以提高</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">30%</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 至</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">100%</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">。我见过对在时间很紧张的情况下或是欠缺经验的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">团队编写出的代码进行优化后，程序运行速度提高了</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">3</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 至</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 倍的情况。不过，通过微调</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">代码让程序的运行速度提升</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 多倍几乎是不可能的。但是选择一种更好的算法或是数据</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">结构，则可以将程序的某个特性的性能从慢到无法忍受提升至可发布的状态。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">1.3</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">　优化是没有问题的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">许多关于性能优化的讨论都会首先严正地警告大家：“不要！不要优化！如果确实需要，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">那么请在项目结束时再优化，而且不要做任何非必需的优化。”例如，著名的计算机科学</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">家高德纳曾经这样说过：</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">“不要进行优化”这条建议已经成为了一项编程常识，甚至许多经验丰富的程序员都认为</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">这是毋庸置疑的。他们对性能调优避而不谈。我认为过度推崇这条建议经常被用作两种行</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">为的借口：编程恶习，以及逃避做少量分析以让代码运行得更快。同时我还认为，盲目地</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">接受这条建议会导致浪费大量</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 周期、用户满意度下降，会浪费大量时间重写那些本</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">应从一开始就更加高效的代码。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">注</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">2</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">：</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818"> </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">高德纳教授是著名的计算机科学家，算法与程序设计技术的先驱者、斯坦福大学计算机系荣休教授、</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">计算机排版系统</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">TEX</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">METAFONT</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818"> 字体系统的发明人，因诸多成就以及大量富于创造力和具有深</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">远影响的著作而誉满全球。</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">——</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">译者注</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">注</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">3</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">：</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818"> </span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:8.00pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">ACM Computing Surveys</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818"> 是美国计算机协会的期刊。——译者注</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">注</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">4</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">：</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818"> CiteSeerX</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818"> 是</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">NEC</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818"> 研究院在自动引文索引（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">Autonomous Citation Indexing</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">，</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">ACI</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">）机制的基础上建设的</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">一个学术论文数字图书馆。</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">——</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">译者注</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">注</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">5</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">：</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818"> </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">威廉</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:7.00pt;color:#181818">•</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818"> 沃尔夫是著名的计算机科学家，因在编程语言以及编译器上的成就而闻名。他曾是弗吉尼亚大</span>
<span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">学的教授和</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">AT&amp;T</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818"> 的教授。</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">——</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">译者注</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">我们应当忘记小的性能改善，百分之九十七的情况下，过早优化都是万恶之源。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">——高德纳</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:5.54pt;color:#181818">2</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">Structured Programming with go to Statements</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">，</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">ACM Computing  </span>

<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:5.54pt;color:#181818">4</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">: 10.1.1.103.6084 </span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">http://citeseerx.ist.psu.edu/viewdoc/summary?doi=10.1.1.103.6084</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Surveys</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:5.54pt;color:#181818">3 </span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">6(4), December 1974, p268. CiteSeerX</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">威廉</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Bold';font-size:7.00pt;font-weight:bold;color:#181818">•</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 沃尔夫</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:5.54pt;color:#181818">5</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">曾说过：</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">以（没有必要达成的）效率之名犯下的计算之罪比其他任何一个原因（包括盲目</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">愚蠢）都多。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">——</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">A Case Against the GOTO</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">，第</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">25</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 届美国</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">ACM</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 会议论文集</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> </span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1972</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）：</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 796</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">优化概述</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">｜</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   3</span>

---

## Page 27

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">我的建议是不要过于教条。优化是没有问题的。学习高效的编程惯用法并在程序中实践之</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">是没有问题的，即使你不知道哪部分代码的性能很重要。这些惯用法对</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 程序很有帮</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">助。使用这些技巧也不会让你被同事鄙夷。如果有人问你为什么不写一些“简单”和低效</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">的代码，你可以这么回答他：“编写高效代码与编写低效无用的代码所需的时间是一样的，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">为什么还会有人特意去编写低效的代码呢？”</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">但是，如果你不清楚重要性，因为不确定哪个算法更好而导致许多天过去了项目仍毫无进</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">展，这是不行的。你因为猜测某段代码有严格的执行时间的要求，就花费数周时间去编写</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">汇编代码，然后将代码作为函数被调用（而实际上</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 编译器可能已经将函数内联展开</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">了），这是不行的。当你实际上并不知道</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 是否真的更快以及</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 是否真的不快时，仅仅</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">因为“大家都知道</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 更快”，就要求你的团队在</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 程序中使用</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 语言编写部分代码，这</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">是不行的。换言之，所有软件开发的最佳实践依然都是适用的。优化并不能成为打破这些</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">规则的理由。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">不知道性能问题出在哪里就花费很多时间进行优化，这是不行的。在第</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">3</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章中我将介绍</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">“</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">90/10</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 规则”。这条规则指出程序中只有</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10%</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的代码的性能是很重要的。因此，试图修改</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">程序中的每条语句去改善程序性能没有必要，也不会有作用。既然只有</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10%</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的代码会对程</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">序的性能产生显著的影响，那么试图随机找出一个性能改善切入点的概率就会很低。第</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">3</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">章会讲解如何使用一些工具帮助大家定位代码中的“热点”。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">当我还在读大学时，我的教授曾经警告我们，最优算法的启动性能开销可能比简单算法更</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">大，因此，应当只在大型数据集上使用它们。可能对于某些冷僻的算法来说确实如此，但</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">根据我的经验，对于简单的查找和排序任务而言，最优算法的准备时间很少，即使在小型</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">数据集上使用它们也能改善性能。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">我也曾经被建议在开发程序时随便使用一种最容易实现的算法，之后在发现程序运行得太</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">慢时，再回过头来优化它。不可否认，这对于推进项目持续进展是一条好的建议，但是一</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">旦你已经编写过几次最优查找或排序的算法了，那么与编写低效的算法相比，编写最优算</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">法并不会更难。而且你也可以在初次编写算法时就正确地实现并调试一种算法，这样以后</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">就可以复用它了。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">实际上，常识可能是性能改善最大的敌人。例如，“每个人都知道”最优排序算法的时间</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">复杂度是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">O</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">n</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> log </span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">n</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">)</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">，其中</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">n</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 是数据集的大小（参见</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">5.1</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 节中关于大</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">O</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 符号和时间开销的简</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">单回顾）。这条常识非常有价值，甚至让开发人员不相信他们的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">O</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">n</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:5.54pt;color:#181818">2</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">)</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 插入排序（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">insertion </span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">sort</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）算法是最优的，但如果它阻止了开发人员查阅文献得出以下发现就不好了：基数排</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">序（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">radix sort</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:5.54pt;color:#181818">6</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">算法的时间复杂度是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">O</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">n</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> log</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:5.54pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">r</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">n</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">) </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（其中</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">r</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 是基数或用于排序的桶的数量），处</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">理速度更快；对于随机分布的数据，</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">ﬂashsort</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 算法的时间复杂度是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">O</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">n</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">)</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">，处理速度更快；</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">还有快速排序算法，根据常识人们将它作为测量其他排序算法性能的测试基准，但在最坏</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">的情况下，它的时间复杂度是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">O</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">n</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:5.54pt;color:#181818">7</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">。亚里士多德曾经误认为“女人的牙齿比男人少”（出</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">自《动物志》第二卷第一部分，</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">http://classics.mit.edu/Aristotle/history_anim.2.ii.html</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">），这个</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">公认的观点让人们信奉了</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1500</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 年，直到有人非常好奇，数了几张嘴中的牙齿数。常识的</span>

<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:5.54pt;color:#181818">2</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">)</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">注</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">6</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">：</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818"> </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">基数排序算法也被称为</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">“</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">桶排法</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">”</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">，它会将要排序的元素分配至某些</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">“</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">桶</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">”</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">中。</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">——</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">译者注</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">注</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">7</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">：</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818"> </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">快速排序算法的时间复杂度最优为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:8.00pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">O</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:8.00pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">n</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818"> log </span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:8.00pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">n</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">)</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">，最坏为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:8.00pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">O</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">(</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:8.00pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">n</span>
<span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">4   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">｜</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">第</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1</span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章</span>

<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:4.66pt;color:#181818">2</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">)</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">。</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">——</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">译者注</span>

---

## Page 28

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">“解毒剂”是实验形式的科学方法。在第</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">3</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章中我们将利用工具测量软件性能，并通过实</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">验验证优化效果。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">在软件开发的世界中，还有一条常识：优化是不重要的。这条常识的理由是，尽管现在代</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">码运行得很慢，但是每年都会有更快的处理器被研发出来，随着时间的推移，它们会免费</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">帮你解决性能问题。就像大多数常识一样，这种想法完全错误。在</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">20</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 世纪</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">80</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 年代和</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">90</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">年代，这种想法似乎看起来是正确的。那时，桌面电脑和独立的应用程序占领了软件开发</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">领域，而且单核处理器的处理速度每</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">18</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 个月就翻一倍。虽然总的看来，如今多核处理器</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">的性能不断强大，但是单个核心的性能增长却非常缓慢，甚至有时还有所下降。如今的程</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">序还必须运行于移动平台上，电池的电量和散热都制约了指令的执行速率。而且，尽管随</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">着时间的推移，会给新客户带来更快的计算机，但是也无法改善现有硬件的性能。现有客</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">户的工作负载随着时间的推移在不断地增加。你的公司为现有客户提高处理速度的唯一办</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">法是发布性能优化后的新版本。优化可以让程序永远保持活力。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">1.4</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">　这儿一纳秒</span><span style="font-family:'SimHei';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">，</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">那儿一纳秒</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">这儿</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 亿，那儿</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 亿，很快就该说到真的钱了。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">桌面电脑的处理速度快得惊人，它们能够每纳秒（或者以更快的速度）分发一条指令，这可是</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">每</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10</span>
<span style="font-family:'SymbolMT';font-size:5.54pt;color:#181818">-</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:5.54pt;color:#181818">9</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 秒啊！这很容易让人误以为当计算机的性能如此强劲时，性能优化可能就无所谓了。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">这种思考方式的问题在于，处理器的处理速度越快，被浪费的指令的累积速度也会越快。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">如果一个程序所执行的指令中</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">50%</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 都是不必要的，那么不管这些不必要的指令的执行速度</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">有多快，只要删除这些指令，程序的处理速度就会变为原来的两倍。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">那些说“性能无所谓”的同事也可能是想说性能对于某些特殊的应用程序——例如受人体</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">反应约束或运行于处理器速度极快的桌面计算机上的应用程序——无所谓。但对于那些运</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">行于内存、电源或者处理速度受限的小型嵌入式设备和移动处理器上的应用程序来说，性</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">能的影响非常大；对于那些运行于大型计算机上的服务器程序的影响也非常大。总而言</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">之，性能对那些必须争夺极其有限的计算资源（内存、电源、</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 周期）的应用程序的影</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">响非常大。同样，只要工作负载很大以至于需要进行分布式处理时，性能的影响就会非常</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">大。在这种情况下，性能的差距会决定到底是需要</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">100</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 台服务器或云实例，还是需要</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">500</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">台或</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1000</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 台。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">尽管计算机的性能在近</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">50</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 年提高了</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">6</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 个数量级，但是这里我仍然要讨论优化。以史为鉴，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">在未来优化仍然非常重要。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">1.5</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">　</span><span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">代码优化策略总结</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">围捕惯犯。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">——常被误认为出自参议员</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Everett Dirkson</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1898</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">—</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1969</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">），但他宣称自己从</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">未说过这句话，虽然他承认说过许多类似的话</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">——路易斯</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:7.00pt;color:#181818">•</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 雷诺上尉（克劳德</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:7.00pt;color:#181818">•</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 雷恩斯饰演），电影《卡萨布兰卡》，</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1942</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 年</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">优化概述</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">｜</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   5</span>

---

## Page 29

<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的混合特性为我们提供了多种实现方式，一方面可以实现性能管理的全自动化，另一</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">方面也可以对性能进行更加精准的控制。正是这些选择方式，使得优化</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 程序以满足性</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">能需求成为可能。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 有一些热点代码是性能“惯犯”，其中包括函数调用、内存分配和循环。下面是一份</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">改善</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 程序性能的方法的总结，也是本书的大纲。这些优化建议简单得让人震惊，而且</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">所有这些建议都是曾经发表过的。当然，恶魔隐藏在细节中。本书的示例和启发将会帮助</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">读者在优化机会出现时更好地把握住它们。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">1.5.1</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">　用好的编译器并用好编译器</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 编译器是非常复杂的软件构件。每种编译器为</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 语句生成的机器码都有差别。它们</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">所看到的优化机会是不同的，会为相同的源代码产生不同的可执行文件。如果打算为代码</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">做出最后一丁点性能提升，那么你可以尝试一下各种不同的编译器，看看是否有一种编译</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">器会为你产生更快的可执行文件。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">关于如何选择</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 编译器的一条最重要的建议，是使用</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">支持</span><span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++11</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的编译器</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">。</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++11</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 实</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">现了右值引用（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">rvalue reference</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）和移动语义（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">move semantics</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">），可以省去许多在以前的</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 版本中无法避免的复制操作（我会在</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">6.6</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 节讨论移动语义）。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">有时，用好的编译器也意味着用好编译器。例如，如果应用程序非常缓慢，那么你应当检</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">查是否打开了编译器的优化选项。这条建议看似非常明显，但是我已经记不清有多少次我</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">向其他人提出这个建议后，他们都承认在编译时确实忘记打开优化选项了。多数情况下，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">只要正确地打开了优化选项，你都不用做额外的优化，因为编译器就可以让程序的运行速</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">度提高数倍。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">默认情况下，许多编译器都不会进行任何优化，因为如果不进行优化，编译器就可以稍微</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">缩短一点编译时间。这一点在</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">20</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 世纪</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">90</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 年代曾经非常重要，但是如今的编译器和计算机</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">已经足够快了，以至于因优化而产生的额外的编译时间开销微不足道。当关闭优化选项</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">时，调试也会变得更加简单，因为程序的执行流程与源代码完全一致。优化选项可能会将</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">代码移出循环、移除一些函数调用和完全移除一些变量。当编译选项打开后，有些编译器</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">将不会生成任何调试符号。虽然部分编译器可能仍然会生成调试符号，但是开发人员想通</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">过在调试器中观察执行流程来理解程序正在做什么就会变得非常困难。许多编译器在调试</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">构建时允许打开和关闭个别不会过多干扰调试的优化选项。仅仅是打开函数内联优化选项</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">就可以显著地提升</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 程序的性能，因为编写许多小的成员函数去访问各个类的成员变量</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">是一种优秀的</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 编码风格。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 编译器的文档对可用优化选项和预处理指令做了全面说明。这份文档如同你在购买新</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">车时获取的操作手册一样——你完全可以不看操作手册就直接坐上并驾驶你的新车，但是</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">其中可能包含了大量的能够帮助你更高效地使用这个庞大、复杂的工具的信息。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">如果你正在</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 或者</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 上开发</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">x86</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 体系结构的应用程序，那么你很幸运，因为有</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">一些非常棒的编译器适合你，而且这些编译器的开发和维护也处于非常活跃的状态。在本</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">书问世的前五年，微软将</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Visual C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 升级了三个版本。每年</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">GCC</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 也会发布不止一个版本。</span>
<span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">6   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">｜</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">第</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1</span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章</span>
