## Page 30

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">在</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">2016</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 年早期，大家一致认为无论是在</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 上还是在</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 上，英特尔的</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 编译</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">器编译出来的代码的速度都最快；虽然</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">GNU</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 编译器</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">GCC</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 编译出的代码的速度稍</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">慢，但是非常符合标准；而微软的</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Visual C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 则折中。虽然我乐于绘制一张图表来说明</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">英特尔</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 编译器产生的代码比</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">GCC</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 快很多，以此来帮助你选择编译器，但这取决于你</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">的代码以及哪家厂商或是组织又发布了一个提升效率的升级版本。虽然购买英特尔</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">编译器需要花费</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1000</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 多美元，但它有</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">30</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 天的免费试用期。</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Visual C++ Express</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 是免费的。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 上的</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">GCC</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 是永久免费的。因此，对你的代码进行一项实验，试试各种编译器可以带</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">来多大的性能提升，其成本并不高。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">1.5.2</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">　使用更好的算法</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">选择一个最优算法对性能优化的效果最大。各种优化手段都能改善程序的性能。它们可以</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">压缩以前看似低效的代码的执行时间，就像通过升级</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">PC</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 能让程序运行得更快一样。但不</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">幸的是，如同升级</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">PC</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 一样，大部分优化手段只能使程序性能呈线性提升。许多优化手段</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">可以将程序性能提升</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">30%</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 至</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">100%</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">。如果足够幸运，也许你可以将性能提升至三倍。但是</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">除非你能找到一种更加高效的算法，否则要想实现性能的指数级增长通常是不太可能的。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">让我们回到</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">8</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 英寸软盘和</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1MHz</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 处理器的时代。某位开发人员设计了一个程序来管理</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">电台。这个程序的功能之一是每天生成一份日志，其中记录了排好序的当天播放过的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">歌曲。问题是这个程序需要大约</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">27</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 小时才能将一天的数据排序完毕，很明显，这让人</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">无法接受。为了让这个重要的排序处理能够运行得更快，这位开发人员诉诸于“英雄</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">壮举”。他使用逆向工程破解了计算机，通过文档上没有写明的方式侵入了微代码，之</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">后编写微代码实现了在内存中进行排序，将程序运行时间减少到了</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">17</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 小时。但</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">17</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 个</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">小时仍然太长了。最后他绝望了，打电话给计算机制造商（也就是我曾经工作过的公</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">司）求助。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">我问这位开发人员他使用的是什么排序算法，他说是</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">归并排序</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Merge Sort</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）。归并排</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">序位于最优比较排序算法之列。那么他对多少条记录排序呢？他回答说“几千条”。这</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">说不通，他所使用的系统应该可以在一个小时之内完成对数据排序。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">我让这位开发人员描述了算法的具体细节。我已经记不清接下来他说的那些折磨人的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">话了，不过我发现了他实现的是插入排序。插入排序是一个非常糟糕的选择，排序所</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">需时间与记录数的平方成正比（请参考</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">5.4.1</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 节）。他知道有种叫作“归并排序”的最</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">优算法。但他却用</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Merge</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Sort</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 两个单词描述出插入算法。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">我使用真正的归并排序为这位顾客编写了一个非常普通的排序例程，这个例程只需要</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">45</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 分钟就可以完成他的数据排序。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">“英勇”地去优化一个糟糕的算法很愚蠢。对代码优化而言，学习和使用查找和排序的最</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">优算法才是康庄大道。一个低效的查找或排序算法的例程可以完全占用一个程序的运行时</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">间。修改代码可以将程序运行时间减少一半。但是替换一种更优的算法后，数据集越大，</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:11.00pt;color:#181818">优化战争故事</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">优化概述</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">｜</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   7</span>

---

## Page 31

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">可以缩短的运行时间就越多。即使在一个只有一打数据的小数据集上，如果频繁查找数</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">据，最优的查找或排序算法也可以帮你节省很多时间。第</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">5</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章将带读者认识最优算法。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">最优算法适用于大大小小的各种程序，从精简的闭式计算到短小的关键字查找函数，再</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">到复杂的数据结构和大规模的程序。市面上有许多优秀的图书讨论了这个主题。开发人员</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">在职业生涯中都应该不断学习这些知识。很遗憾，在本书中我只能对优化算法主题浅谈</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">辄止。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">5.5</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 节将讲解几个改善程序性能的重要技巧，其中包括</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">预计算</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">precomputation</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">，将计算从</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">运行时移动至链接、编译或是设计时）、</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">延迟计算</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">lazy computation</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">，如果通常计算结果</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">不会被使用，那么将计算推迟至真正需要使用计算结果时）和</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">缓存</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">caching</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">，节省和复用</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">昂贵的计算）。第</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">7</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章会使用很多示例来实践这些技巧。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">1.5.3</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">　使用更好的库</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 编译器提供的标准</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 模板库和运行时库必须是可维护的、全面的和非常健壮的。令</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">开发人员吃惊的是，我们无需对这些库进行调优。可能更令人吃惊的是，虽然</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 已经发</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">明出来</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">30</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 年多了，商业</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 编译器的库仍然有</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">bug</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">，而且可能不遵循现在的</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 标准，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">甚至不遵循编译器发布时的标准。这使得测量和推荐优化方法的任务变得非常复杂，也使</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">得开发人员认为没有任何优化经验是可以移植的。第</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">8</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章将讨论这些问题。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">对进行性能优化的开发人员来说，掌握标准</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 模板库是必需的技能。本书对查找和排序</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">算法（第</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">9</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章）、容器类的最优惯用法（第</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章）</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">、</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">I/O</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（第</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">11</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章）、并发（第</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">12</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章）和</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">内存管理（第</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">13</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章）提出了一些优化建议。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">有一些开源库实现了非常重要的功能，如内存管理（请参见</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">13.2</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 节）。它们提供的复杂的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">实现可能比供应商提供的</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 运行时库更快、更强。这些可供选择的开源库的一个优势</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">是，它们很容易地整合至现有的工程中，并能够立即改善程序性能。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Boost Project</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">http://www.boost.org</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）和</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Google Code</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">https://code.google.com</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）等公开了很</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">多可供使用的库，其中有一些用于</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">I/O</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">、窗口、处理字符串（请参见</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">4.3.3</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 节）和并发（请</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">参见</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">12.5</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 节）的库。它们虽然不是标准库的替代品，却可以帮助我们改善性能和加入新的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">特性。这些库在设计上的权衡与标准库不同，从而获得了处理速度上的提升。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">最后，开发人员还可以开发适合自己项目的库，通过放松标准库中的某些安全性和健壮性</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">约束来换取更快的运行速度。我会在第</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">8</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章中讲解以上这些内容。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">某些方式的函数调用的开销非常大（请参见</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">7.2.1</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 节）。优秀的函数库的</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">API</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 所提供的函数</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">反映了这些</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">API</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的惯用法，使得用户可以无需频繁地调用其中的基础函数。例如，如果一</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">个用于获取字符的</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">API</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 只提供了</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">get_char()</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 函数，那么用户在获取每个字符时都需要进行</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">一次函数调用。而如果这个</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">API</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 同时提供一个</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">get_buffer()</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 函数，就可以避免在获取每个</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">字符时都发生昂贵的函数调用开销。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">要想隐藏高度优化后的程序的复杂性，函数和类库是非常合适的地方。作为调用库的回</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">报，它们会以最高的效率完成工作。库函数通常位于深层嵌套调用链的底端，在那里，性</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">能改善的效果会更加明显。</span>
<span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">8   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">｜</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">第</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1</span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章</span>

<span style="font-family:'MicrosoftYaHei';font-size:8.00pt;color:#b4b4b4">图灵社区会员 ChenyangGao(2339083510@qq.com) 专享 尊重版权</span>

---

## Page 32

<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">1.5.4</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">　减少内存分配和复制</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">减少对内存管理器的调用是一种非常有效的优化手段，以至于开发人员只要掌握了这一个</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">技巧就可以变为成功的性能优化人员。绝大多数</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 语言特性的性能开销最多只是几个指</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">令，但是每次调用内存管理器的开销却是数千个指令。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">由于字符串是许多</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 程序中非常重要（和性能开销大）的部分，我用了整整一章将其作</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">为优化手段的案例分析。第</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">4</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章中介绍和引导出了许多在大家所熟知的字符串处理背景下</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">的优化概念。第</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">6</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章将讲解如何既减少动态内存分配的性能开销又不放弃实用的</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 编程</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">惯用法，比如字符串和标准库容器。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">对缓存复制函数的一次调用也可能消耗数千个</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 周期。因此，很明显减少复制是一种</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">提高代码运行速度的优化方式。大量复制的发生都与内存分配有关，所以修改一处往往也</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">会消灭另一处。其他可能会发生复制的热点代码是构造函数和赋值运算符以及输入输出。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">第</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">6</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章将讨论这个主题。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">1.5.5</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">　移除计算</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">除了内存分配和函数调用外，单条</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 语句的性能开销通常都很小。但是如果在循环中</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">执行</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">100</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 万次这条语句，或是每次程序处理事件时都执行这条语句，那么这就是个大问题</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">了。绝大多数程序都会有一个或多个主要的事件处理循环和一个或多个处理字符的函数。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">找出并优化这些循环几乎总是可以让性能优化硕果累累。第</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">7</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章提出了一些帮助你找出频</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">繁被执行的语句的建议，你会发现这些语句几乎总是位于循环处理中。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">以性能优化为主题的文献介绍了许多高效地使用单独的</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 语句的技巧。许多程序员相信</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">这些诀窍是优化的基础。这种看法的问题在于，除非一段代码真的是热点代码（被频繁地</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">执行的代码），否则从中移除一两句内存访问对程序的整体性能不会有什么改善。第</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">3</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">将介绍在尝试减少计算数量之前，如何确定程序中的哪部分会被频繁地执行。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">同时，现代</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 编译器在进行这些局部改善方面也做得非常优秀了。因此，开发人员不</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">应当有强迫症，将大段代码中的出现的</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">i++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 都换成</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">++i</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">，或是展开所有的循环，不遗余力</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">地向每位同事讲解什么是</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">达夫设备</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Duff</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">’</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">s Device</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:5.54pt;color:#181818">8</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">以及它的优点。当然，我仍然会在第</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">7</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">章简单地介绍一下这些技巧。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">1.5.6</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">　使用更好的数据结构</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">选择最合适的数据结构对性能有着深刻的影响，因为插入、迭代、排序和检索元素的算法</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">的运行时开销取决于数据结构。除此之外，不同的数据结构在使用内存管理器的方式上也</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">有所不同。另一个原因是数据结构可能有也可能没有优秀的缓存本地化。第</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章将探索</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 标准库提供的数据结构的性能、行为和权衡。第</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">9</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章将讨论使用标准库算法去实现基</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">于简单矢量和</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 数组的表数据结构。</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">注</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">8</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">：</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818"> </span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">由汤姆</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:7.00pt;color:#181818">•</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818"> 达夫在卢卡斯影业工作时所设计的循环展开方法。</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">——译者注</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">优化概述</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">｜</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   9</span>

<span style="font-family:'MicrosoftYaHei';font-size:8.00pt;color:#b4b4b4">图灵社区会员 ChenyangGao(2339083510@qq.com) 专享 尊重版权</span>

---

## Page 33

<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">1.5.7</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">　提高并发性</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">大多数程序都需要等待发生在物理现实世界中的无聊、慢吞吞的活动完成。它们必须等待</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">文件从硬盘上读取完成、网页从互联中返回或者是用户的手指缓慢地按下键盘。任何时</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">候，如果一个程序的处理进度因需要等待这些事件被暂停，而没有利用这些时间进行其他</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">处理，都是一种浪费。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">现代计算机都可以使用多个处理核心来执行指令。如果一项工作被分给几个处理器执行，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">那么它可以更快地执行完毕。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">伴随并发执行而来的是用于同步并发线程让它们可以共享数据的工具。有人可以用好这些</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">工具，有人则用不好。第</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">12</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章探讨了如何高效地控制并发线程同步。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">1.5.8</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">　优化内存管理</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">内存管理器作为</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 运行时库中的一部分，管理着动态内存分配。它在许多</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 程序中</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">都会被频繁地执行。</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 确实为内存管理提供了丰富的</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">API</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">，虽然多数开发人员都从来没</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">有使用过。第</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">13</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章将展示一些改善内存管理效率的技术。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">1.6</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">　小结</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">本书将帮助开发人员识别和利用以下优化机会来改善代码性能。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">使用更好的编译器，打开编译选项</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">使用最优算法</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">使用更好的库并用好库</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">减少内存分配</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">减少复制</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">移除计算</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">使用最优数据结构</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">提高并发</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">优化内存管理</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">正如我之前所说过的，恶魔隐藏在细节中。让我们进入正题吧。</span>

<span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">｜</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">第</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1</span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章</span>

<span style="font-family:'MicrosoftYaHei';font-size:8.00pt;color:#b4b4b4">图灵社区会员 ChenyangGao(2339083510@qq.com) 专享 尊重版权</span>

## Page 34

<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">撒谎，即讲述美丽而不真实的故事，乃是艺术的真正目的。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">本章的目的是为读者提供与本书中所描述的优化技术相关的计算机硬件的最基本的背景知</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">识，这样读者就不必疯狂地研究那</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">600</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 多页的处理器手册了。本章我们将简单地了解处理</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">器的体系结构，从中获得性能优化的启发。虽然本章中的信息非常重要且实用，但迫不及</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">待地想学习优化技术的读者可以先跳过本章，当在后面的章节中遇到本章中的知识时再回</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">过头来学习。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">如今所使用的微处理器设备的种类多样，从只有几千个逻辑门且时钟频率低于</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1MHz</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的价</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">值</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 美元的嵌入式设备，到有数十亿逻辑门且时钟频率达到千兆赫兹级别的桌面级设备。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">一台包含数千个独立执行单元的大型计算机的尺寸可以与一个大房间相当，它消耗的电力</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">足够点亮一座小城市中所有的电灯。这很容易让人误以为这些种类繁多的计算设备之间的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">联系不具有一般性。</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">但事实上，它们之间是有可利用的相似点的。毕竟，如果没有任何相</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">似点的话，编译器就无法为这么多处理器编译</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 代码了。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">所有这些被广泛使用的计算机都会执行存储在内存中的指令。指令所操作的数据也是存</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">储在内存中的。内存被分为许多小的</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">字</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">word</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">），这些字由若干</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">位</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">bit</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）组成。其中一</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">小部分宝贵的内存字是</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">寄存器</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">register</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">），它们的名字被直接定义在机器指令中。其他</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">绝大多数内存字则都是以数值型的</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">地址</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">address</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）命名的。每台计算机中都有一个特</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">殊的寄存器保存着下一条待执行的指令的地址。如果将内存看作一本书，那么</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">执行地</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">址</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">execution address</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）就相当于指向要阅读的下一个单词的手指。</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">执行单元</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">execution </span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">unit</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">，也被称为处理器、核心、</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">、运算器等其他名字）从内存中读取指令流，然后执</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">行它们。指令会告诉执行单元要从内存中读取（加载，取得）什么数据，如何处理数据，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">以及将什么结果写入（存储、保存）到内存中。计算机是由遵守物理定律的设备组成的。</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYe3gj';font-size:19.00pt;color:#181818">第</span><span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:19.00pt;color:#181818">2</span><span style="font-family:'HYe3gj';font-size:19.00pt;color:#181818"> 章</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYb2gj';font-size:26.83pt;color:#181818">影响优化的计算机行为</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">——奥斯卡</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:7.00pt;color:#181818">•</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 王尔德，“谎言的衰朽”，《意图集》，</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1891</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 年</span>

<span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">11</span>

![](./C++性能优化指南 (甘瑟尔罗斯) (Z-Library)_assets/images/p034_img01.png)

---

## Page 35

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">从内存地址读取数据和向内存地址写入数据是需要花费时间的，指令对数据进行操作也</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">是需要花费时间的。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">除了这条基本原则外，就如每个计算机专业新生都知道的，计算机体系结构的“族谱”也</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">会不断地扩大。因为计算机体系结构是易变的，所以很难严格地测量出硬件行为在数值上</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">的规律。现代处理器做了许多不同的、交互的事情来提高指令执行速度，导致指令的执行</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">时间实际上变得难以确定。还有一个问题是，许多开发人员甚至无法准确地知道他们的代</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">码会运行在什么处理器上，多数情况下只能用试探法。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">2.1</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">　</span><span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">所相信的计算机谎言</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">当然，</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 程序至少会假装相信上节中讲解过的简单的计算机基本模型中的一个版本。其</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">中有可以以固定字符长度的字节为单位寻址，在本质上容量是无限的内存。有一个与其他</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">任何有效的内存地址都不同的特殊的地址，叫作</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">nullptr</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">。整数</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">0</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 会被转换为</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">nullptr</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">，尽</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">管在地址</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">0</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 上不需要</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">nullptr</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">。有一个概念上的执行地址指向正在被执行的源代码语句。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">各条语句会按照编写顺序执行，受到</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 控制流程语句的控制。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 知道计算机远比这个简单模型要复杂。它在这台闪闪发亮的机器下提供了一些快</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">速功能。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 程序只需要表现得好像语句是按照顺序执行的。</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 编译器和计算机自身只要能</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">够确保每次计算的含义都不会改变，就可以改变执行顺序使程序运行得更快。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">自</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++11</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 开始，</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 不再认为只有一个执行地址。</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 标准库现在支持启动和终止线</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">程以及同步线程间的内存访问。在</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++11</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">之前，</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">程序员对</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 编译器隐瞒了他们的线程，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">有时候这会导致难以调试。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">某些内存地址可能是设备寄存器，而不是普通内存。这些地址的值可能会在同一个</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">线程对该地址的两次连续读的间隔发生变化，这表示硬件发生了变化。在</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 中用</span>
<span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">volatile</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 关键字定义这些地址。声明一个</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">volatile</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 变量会要求编译器在每次使用该变</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">量时都获取它的一份新的副本，而不用通过将该变量的值保存在一个寄存器中并复用它</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">来优化程序。另外，也可以声明指向</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">volatile</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 内存的指针。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• C++11</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 提供了一个名为</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">std::atomic&lt;&gt;</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的特性，可以让内存在一段短暂的时间内表现得</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">仿佛是字节的简单线性存储一样，这样可以远离所有现代处理器的复杂性，包括多线程</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">执行、多层高速缓存等。有些开发人员误以为这与</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">volatile</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 是一样的，其实他们错了。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">操作系统也欺骗了程序和用户。实际上，操作系统的目的就是为了给每个程序讲一个让它</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">们信服的谎言。最重要的谎言之一是，操作系统希望每个程序都相信它们是独立运行于计</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">算机上的，而且这些计算机的内存是无限的，还有无限的处理器来运行程序的所有线程。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">操作系统会使用计算机硬件来隐藏这些谎言，这样</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 不得不相信它们。除了降低程序的运</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">行速度外，这些谎言其实对程序运行并没有什么影响。不过，它们会导致性能测量变得复杂。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">2.2</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">　计算机的真相</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">只有最简单的微处理器和某些具有悠久历史的大型机才直接与</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 模型相符。对性能优化</span>
<span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">12   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">｜</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">第</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">2</span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章</span>

---

## Page 36

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">而言非常重要的是，真实计算机的实际内存硬件的处理速度与指令的执行速率相比是很慢</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">的。内存并非真的是以字节为单位被访问的，内存并非是一个由相同元素组成的简单的线</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">性数组，而且它的容量也是有限的。真实的计算机可能有不止一个指令地址。真实的计算</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">机非常快，但并非因为它们执行指令非常快，而是因为它们同时执行许多指令，而且它们</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">内部的复杂电路可以确保这些同时执行的指令表现得就像一个接一个地执行一样。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">2.2.1</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">　内存很慢</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">计算机的主内存相对于它内部的逻辑门和寄存器来说非常慢。将电子从微处理器芯片中注入</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">相对广阔的一块铜制电路板上的电路，然后将其沿着电路推到几厘米外的内存芯片中，这个</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">过程所花费的时间为电子穿越微处理器内各个独立的微距晶体管所需时间的数千倍。主内存</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">太慢，所以桌面级处理器在从主内存中读取一个数据字的时间内，可以执行数百条指令。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">优化的根据在于处理器访问内存的开销远比其他开销大，包括执行指令的开销。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">通往主内存的接口是限制执行速度的瓶颈。这个瓶颈甚至有一个名字，叫冯</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:7.00pt;color:#181818">•</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 诺伊曼</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">瓶颈。它是以著名的计算机体系结构先锋和数学家约翰</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:7.00pt;color:#181818">•</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 冯</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:7.00pt;color:#181818">•</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 诺伊曼（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1903</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">—</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1957</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">名字命名的。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">例如，一台使用主频为</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1000MHz</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">DDR2</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 内存设备的个人计算机（几年前典型的计</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">算机，容易计算其性能），其理论带宽是每秒</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">20</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 亿字，也就是每字</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">500</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 皮秒（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">ps</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）。但</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">这并不意味着这台计算机每</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">500</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 皮秒就可以读或写一个随机的数据字。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">首先，只有顺序访问才能在一个周期内完成（相当于频率为</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1000MHz</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的时钟的半个时</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">标）。而访问一个非连续的位置则会花费</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">6</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 至</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 个周期。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">多个活动会争夺对内存总线的访问。处理器会不断地读取包含下一条需要执行的指</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">令的内存。高速缓存控制器会将数据内存块保存至高速缓存中，刷新已写的缓存行。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">DRAM</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 控制器还会“偷用”周期刷新内存中的动态</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">RAM</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 基本存储单元的电荷。多核</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">处理器的核心数量足以确保内存总线的通信数据量是饱和的。数据从主内存读取至某</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">个核心的实际速率大概是每字</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">20</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 至</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">80</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 纳秒（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">ns</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">根据摩尔定律，每年处理器核心的数量都会增加。但是这也无法让连接主内存的接口</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">变快。因此，未来核心数量成倍地增加，对性能的改善效果却是递减的。这些核心只</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">能等待访问内存的机会。上述对性能的隐式限制被称为</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">内存墙</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">memory wall</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">2.2.2</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">　内存访问并非以字节为单位</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">虽然</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 认为每个字节都是可以独立访问的，但计算机会通过获取更大块的数据来补偿缓</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">慢的内存速度。最小型的处理器可以每次从主内存中获取</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 字节，桌面级处理器则可以立</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">即获取</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">64</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 字节。一些超级计算机和图形处理器还可以获取更多。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">当</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 获取一个多字节类型的数据，比如一个</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">int</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">、</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">double</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 或者指针时，构成数据的字</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:11.00pt;color:#181818">冯</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Bold';font-size:7.00pt;font-weight:bold;color:#181818">•</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:11.00pt;color:#181818"> 诺伊曼瓶颈</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">影响优化的计算机行为</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">｜</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   13</span>

<span style="font-family:'MicrosoftYaHei';font-size:8.00pt;color:#b4b4b4">图灵社区会员 ChenyangGao(2339083510@qq.com) 专享 尊重版权</span>

---

## Page 37

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">节可能跨越了两个物理内存字。这种访问被称为</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">非对齐的内存访问</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">unaligned memory </span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">access</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）。此处优化的意义在于，一次非对齐的内存访问的时间相当于这些字节在同一个字</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">中时的两倍，因为需要读取两个字。</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 编译器会帮助我们对齐结构体，使每个字段的起</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">始字节地址都是该字段的大小的倍数。但是这样也会带来相应的问题：结构体的“洞”中</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">包含了无用的数据。在定义结构体时，对各个数据字段的大小和顺序稍加注意，可以在保</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">持对齐的前提下使结构体更加紧凑。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">2.2.3</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">　某些内存访问会比其他的更慢</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">为了进一步补偿主内存的缓慢速度，许多计算机中都有</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">高速缓存</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">cache memory</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">），一种非</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">常接近处理器的快速的、临时的存储，来加快对那些使用最频繁的内存字的访问速度。一</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">些计算机没有高速缓存，其他一些计算机则有一层或多层高速缓存，其中每一层都比前一</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">层更小、更快和更昂贵。当一个执行单元要获取的字节已经被缓存时，无需访问主内存即</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">可立即获得这些字节。高速缓存的速度快多少呢？一种大致的估算经验是，高速缓存层次</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">中每一层的速度大约是它下面一层的</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 倍。在桌面级处理器中，通过一级高速缓存、二</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">级高速缓存、三级高速缓存、主内存和磁盘上的虚拟内存页访问内存的时间开销范围可以</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">跨越五个数量级。这就是专注于指令的时钟周期和其他“奥秘”经常会令人恼怒而且没有</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">效果的一个原因，高速缓存的状态会让指令的执行时间变得非常难以确定。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">当执行单元需要获取不在高速缓存中的数据时，有一些当前处于高速缓存中的数据必须被</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">舍弃以换取足够的空余空间。通常，选择放弃的数据都是最近很少被使用的数据。这一点</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">与性能优化有着紧密的关系，因为这意味着访问那些被频繁地访问过的存储位置的速度会</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">比访问不那么频繁地被访问的存储位置更快。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">读取一个不在高速缓存中的字节甚至会导致许多临近的字节也都被缓存起来（这也意味</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">着，许多当前被缓存的字节将会被舍弃）。这些临近的字节也就可以被高速访问了。对于</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">性能优化而言，这一点非常重要，因为这意味着平均而言，访问内存中相邻位置的字节要</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">比访问互相远隔的字节的速度更快。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">就</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 而言，这表示一个包含循环处理的代码块的执行速度可能会更快。这是因为组成</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">循环处理的指令会被频繁地执行，而且互相紧挨着，因此更容易留在高速缓存中。一段包</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">含函数调用或是含有</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">if</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 语句导致执行发生跳转的代码则会执行得较慢，因为代码中各个</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">独立的部分不会那么频繁地被执行，也不是那么紧邻着。相比紧凑的循环，这样的代码在</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">高速缓存中会占用更多的空间。如果程序很大，而且缓存有限，那么一些代码必须从高速</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">缓存中舍弃以为其他代码腾出空间，当下一次需要这段代码时，访问速度会变慢。类似</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">地，访问包含连续地址的数据结构（如数组或矢量），要比访问包含通过指针链接的节点</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">的数据结构快，因为连续地址的数据所需的存储空间更少。访问包含通过指针链接的记录</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">的数据结构（例如链表或者树）可能会较慢，这是因为需要从主内存读取每个节点的数据</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">到新的缓存行中。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">2.2.4</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">　内存字分为大端和小端</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">处理器可以一次从内存中读取一字节的数据，但是更多时候都会读取由几个连续的字节组</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">成的一个数字。例如，在微软的</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Visual C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 中，读取</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">int</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 值时会读取</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">4</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 字节。由于同一个</span>
<span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">14   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">｜</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">第</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">2</span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章</span>

---

## Page 38

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">内存可以以两种不同的方式访问，设计计算机的人必须面对一个问题：首字节，即最低地</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">址字节，是组成</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">int</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的最高有效位还是最低有效位呢？</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">乍一看，这似乎没什么问题。当然，一台计算机中的所有部件就“最低地址是</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">int</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的哪一</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">端”这一点达成一致是非常重要的，否则就会出现混乱。而且，它们之间的区别是非常明</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">显的。如果</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">int</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 值</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">0x01234567</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 存储在地址</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1000~1003</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 中，而且首先存储小端，那么在地</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">址</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1000</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 中存储的是</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">0x01</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">，在地址</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1003</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 中存储的是</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">0x67</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">。反之，如果首先存储大端，那</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">么在地址</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1000</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 中存储的是</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">0x67</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">，</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">0x01</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 被存储在地址</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1003</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 中。从首字节地址读取最高有</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">效位的计算机被称为</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">大端计算机</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">，</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">小端计算机</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">则会首先读取最低有效位。因为有两种存储</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">整数值（或指针）的方式，而且找不到偏向其中一种的理由，所以工作在不同处理器上的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">不同公司的不同团队的选择可能会不同。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">问题出在当被写至磁盘上的数据或者由一台计算机通过网络传输的数据会被另外一台计算</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">机读取的时候。磁盘和网络一次只传送一字节，而不是整个</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">int</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 值。所以，这关系到哪一</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">端首先被存储或发送。如果发送数据的计算机与接收数据的计算机在这一点上不一致，那</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">么发送的</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">0x01234567</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 则会被接收为</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">0x67452301</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">，导致</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">int</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 值发生了改变。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">字节序</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">endian-ness</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）只是</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 不能指定</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">int</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 中位的存储方式或是设置联合体中的一个字</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">段会如何影响其他字段的原因之一。所编写的程序可以工作于一类计算机上，却在另一类</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">计算机上崩溃，原因也在于字节序。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">2.2.5</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">　内存容量是有限的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">实际上，计算机中的内存容量并非是无限的。为了维持内存容量无限的假象，操作系统可</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">以如同使用高速缓存一样使用物理内存，将没有放入物理内存中的数据作为文件存储在磁</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">盘上。这种机制被称为</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">虚拟内存</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">virtual memory</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）。虚拟内存制造出了拥有充足的物理内</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">存的假象。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">不过，从磁盘上获取一个内存块需要花费数十毫秒，对现代计算机来说，这几乎是一个</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">恒定值。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">想让高速缓存更快是非常昂贵的。一台台式计算机或是手机中可能会有数吉字节的主内存，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">但是只有几百万字节的高速缓存。通常，程序和它们的数据不会被存储在高速缓存中。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">高速缓存和虚拟内存带来的一个影响是，由于高速缓存的存在，在进行性能测试时，一个</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">函数运行于整个程序的上下文中时的执行速度可能是运行于测试套件中时的万分之一。当</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">运行于整个程序的上下文中时，函数和它的数据不太可能存储至缓存中，而在测试套件的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">上下文中，它们则通常会被缓存起来。这个影响放大了减少内存或磁盘使用量带来的优化</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">收益，而减小代码体积的优化收益则没有任何变化。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">第二个影响则是，如果一个大程序访问许多离散的内存地址，那么可能没有足够的高速缓</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">存来保存程序刚刚使用的数据。这会导致一种性能衰退，称为</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">页抖动</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">page thrashing</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）。当</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">在微处理器内部的高速缓存中发生页抖动时，性能会降低；当在操作系统的虚拟缓存文件</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">中发生页抖动时，性能会下降为原来的</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1/1000</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">。过去，计算机的物理内存很少，页抖动更</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">加普遍。不过，如今，这个问题仍然会发生。</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">影响优化的计算机行为</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">｜</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   15</span>

---

## Page 39

<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">2.2.6</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">　指令执行缓慢</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">嵌入在咖啡机和微波炉中的简单的微处理器被设计为执行指令的速度与从内存中获取指令</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">一样快。桌面级微处理器则有额外的资源并发地处理指令，因此它们执行指令的速度可以</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">比从主内存获取指令快很多倍，多数时候都需要高速缓存去“喂饱”它们的执行单元。对</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">优化而言，这意味着内存访问决定了计算开销。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">如果没有其他东西“妨碍”，现代桌面级处理器可以以惊人的速率执行指令。它们每几百</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">皮秒（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 皮秒是</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10</span>
<span style="font-family:'SymbolMT';font-size:5.54pt;color:#181818">-</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:5.54pt;color:#181818">12</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 秒，一段非常非常短的时间）就可以完成一次指令处理。但这并不意</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">味着每条指令只需要皮秒数量级的时间即可执行完毕。处理器中包含一条指令“流水线”，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">它支持并发执行指令。指令在流水线中被解码、获取参数、执行计算，最后保存处理结</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">果。处理器的性能越强大，这条流水线就越复杂。它会将指令分解为若干阶段，这样就可</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">以并发地处理更多的指令。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">如果指令</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">B</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 需要指令</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">A</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的计算结果，那么在计算出指令</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">A</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的处理结果前是无法执行指令</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">B</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">的计算的。这会导致在指令执行过程中发生</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">流水线停滞</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">pipeline stall</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）——一个短暂的暂</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">停，因为两条指令无法完全同时执行。如果指令</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">A</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 需要从内存中获取值，然后进行运算得</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">到线程</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">B</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 所需的值，那么流水线停滞时间会特别长。流水线停滞会拖累高性能微处理器，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">让它变得与烤面包机中的处理器的速度一样慢。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">2.2.7</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">　计算机难以作决定</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">另一个会导致流水线停滞的原因是计算机需要作决定。大多数情况下，在执行完一条指令</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">后，处理器都会获取下一个内存地址中的指令继续执行。这时，多数情况下，下一条指令</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">已经被保存在高速缓存中了。一旦流水线的第一道工序变为可用状态，指令就可以连续地</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">进入到流水线中。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">但是控制转义指令略有不同。跳转指令或跳转子例程指令会将执行地址变为一个新的值。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">在执行跳转指令一段时间后，执行地址才会被更新。在这之前是无法从内存中读取“下</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">一条”指令并将其放入到流水线中的。新的执行地址中的内存字不太可能会存储在高速</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">缓存中。在更新执行地址和加载新的“下一条”指令到流水线中的过程中，会发生流水</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">线停滞。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">在执行了一个条件分支指令后，执行可能会走向两个方向：下一条指令或者分支目标地址</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">中的指令。最终会走向哪个方向取决于之前的某些计算的结果。这时，流水线会发生停</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">滞，直至与这些计算结果相关的全部指令都执行完毕，而且还会继续停滞一段时间，直至</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">决定一下条指令的地址并取得下一条指令为止。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">对性能优化而言，这一项的意义在于计算比做决定更快。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">2.2.8</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">　程序执行中的多个流</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">任何运行于现代操作系统中的程序都会与同时运行的其他程序、检查磁盘或者新的</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Java</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 和</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Flash</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 版本的定期维护进程以及控制网络接口、磁盘、声音设备、加速器、温度计和其他</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">外设的操作系统的各个部分共享计算机。每个程序都会与其他程序竞争计算机资源。</span>
<span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">16   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">｜</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">第</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">2</span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章</span>

---

## Page 40

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">程序不会过多在意这些事情。它只是会运行得稍微慢一点而已。不过有一个例外，那就是</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">当许多程序一齐开始运行，互相竞争内存和磁盘时。为了性能调优，如果一个程序必须在</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">启动时执行或是在负载高峰期时执行，那么在测量性能时也必须带上负载。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">在</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">2016</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 年早期，台式计算机有多达</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">16</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 个处理器核心。手机和平板电脑中的微处理器也有</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">多达</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">8</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 个核心。但是，快速地浏览下</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Windows</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的任务管理器、</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Linux</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的进程状态输出结果</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">和</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Android</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的任务列表就可以发现，微处理器所执行的软件进程远比这个数量大，而且绝</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">大多数进程都有多个线程在执行。操作系统会执行一个线程一段很短的时间，然后将上下</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">文切换至其他线程或进程。对程序而言，就仿佛执行一条语句花费了一纳秒，但执行下一</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">条语句花费了</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">60</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 毫秒。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">切换上下文究竟是什么意思呢？如果操作系统正在将一个线程切换至同一个程序的另外一</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">个线程，这表示要为即将暂停的线程保存处理器中的寄存器，然后为即将被继续执行的线</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">程加载之前保存过的寄存器。现代处理器中的寄存器包含数百字节的数据。当新线程继续</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">执行时，它的数据可能并不在高速缓存中，所以当加载新的上下文到高速缓存中时，会有</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">一个缓慢的初始化阶段。因此，切换线程上下文的成本很高。</span>
