<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">当操作系统从一个程序切换至另外一个程序时，这个过程的开销会更加昂贵。所有脏的高</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">速缓存页面（页面被入了数据，但还没有反映到主内存中）都必须被刷新至物理内存中。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">所有的处理器寄存器都需要被保存。然后，内存管理器中的“物理地址到虚拟地址”的内</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">存页寄存器也需要被保存。接着，新线程的“物理地址到虚拟地址”的内存页寄存器和处</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">理器寄存器被载入。最后就可以继续执行了。但是这时高速缓存是空的，因此在高速缓存</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">被填充满之前，还有一段缓慢且需要激烈地竞争内存的初始化阶段。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">当一个程序必须等某个事件发生时，它甚至可能会在这个事件发生后继续等待，直至操作</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">系统让处理器为继续执行程序做好准备。这会导致当程序运行于其他程序的上下文中，竞</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">争计算机资源时，程序的运行时间变得更长和更加难以确定。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">为了能够达到更好的性能，一个多核处理器的执行单元及相关的高速缓存，与其他的执行</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">单元及相关的高速缓存都是或多或少互相独立的。不过，所有的执行单元都共享同样的主</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">内存。执行单元必须竞争使用那些将可以它们链接至主内存的硬件，使得在拥有多个执行</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">单元的计算机中，冯</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:7.00pt;color:#181818">•</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 诺依曼瓶颈的限制变得更加明显。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">当执行单元写值时，这个值会首先进入高速缓存内存。不过最终，这个值将被写入至主内</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">存中，这样其他所有的执行单元就都可以看见这个值了。但是，这些执行单元在访问主内</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">存时存在着竞争，所以可能在执行单元改变了一个值，然后又执行几百个指令后，主内存</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">中的值才会被更新。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">因此，如果一台计算机有多个执行单元，那么一个执行单元可能需要在很长一段时间后才</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">能看见另一个执行单元所写的数据被反映至主内存中，而且主内存发生改变的顺序可能与</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">指令的执行顺序不一样。受到不可预测的时间因素的干扰，执行单元看到的共享内存字中</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">的值可能是旧的，也可能是被更新后的值。这时，必须使用特殊的同步指令来确保运行于</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">不同执行单元间的线程看到的内存中的值是一致的。对优化而言，这意味着访问线程间的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">共享数据比访问非共享数据要慢得多。</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">影响优化的计算机行为</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">｜</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   17</span>

---

## Page 41

<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">2.2.9</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">　调用操作系统的开销是昂贵的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">除了最小的处理器外，其他处理器都有硬件可以确保程序之间是互相隔离的。这样，程序</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">A</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 不能读写和执行属于程序</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">B</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的物理内存。这个硬件还会保护操作系统内核不会被程序覆</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">写。另一方面，操作系统内核需要能够访问所有程序的内存，这样程序就可以通过系统调</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">用访问操作系统。有些操作系统还允许程序发送访问共享内存的请求。许多系统调用的发</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">生方式和共享内存的分布方式是多样和神秘的。对优化而言，这意味着系统调用的开销是</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">昂贵的，是单线程程序中的函数调用开销的数百倍。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">2.3</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">　</span><span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">也会说谎</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 对用户所撒的最大的谎言就是运行它的计算机的结构是简单的、稳定的。为了假装相</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">信这条谎言，</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 让开发人员不用了解每种微处理器设备的细节即可编程，如同正在使用</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">真实得近乎残酷的汇编语言编程一样。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">2.3.1</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">　并非所有语句的性能开销都相同</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">在</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Kernighan</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Ritchie</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的《</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 程序设计语言》一书中，所有语句的性能开销都一样。一个</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">函数调用可能包含任意复杂的计算。但一个赋值语句通常只是将保存在一个寄存器中的内</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">容变为另外一个内容保存在另一个寄存器中。因此，以下赋值语句</span>
<span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:8.50pt;color:#181818">int i</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.50pt;color:#181818">，</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:8.50pt;color:#181818">j; </span>
<span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:8.50pt;color:#181818"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:8.50pt;color:#181818">... </span>
<span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:8.50pt;color:#181818"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:8.50pt;color:#181818">i = j;</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">会从</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">j</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 中复制</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">2</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 或</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">4</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 字节到</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">i</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 中。所声明的变量类型可能是</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">int</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">、</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">float</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 或</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">struct big </span>
<span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">struct *</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">，但是赋值语句所做的工作量是一样的。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">不过现在，这已经不再是正确的了。在</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 中，将一个</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">int</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 赋值给另外一个</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">int</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的工作量</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">与相应的</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 语言赋值语句的工作量是完全一样的。但是，一个赋值语句，如</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">BigInstance </span>
<span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">i = OtherObject;</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 会复制整个对象的结构。更值得注意的是，这类赋值语句会调用</span>
<span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">BigInstance</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的构造函数，而其中可能隐藏了不确定的复杂性。当一个表达式被传递给一</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">个函数的形参时，也会调用构造函数。当函数返回值时也是一样的。而且，由于算数操作</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">符和比较操作符也可以被重载，所以</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">A=B*C;</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 可能是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">n</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 维矩阵相乘，</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">if (x&lt;y)...</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 可能比较</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">的是具有任意复杂度的有向图中的两条路径。对优化而言，这一点的意义是某些语句隐藏</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">了大量的计算，但从这些语句的外表上看不出它的性能开销会有多大。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">先学习</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的开发人员不会对此感到惊讶。但是对那些先学习</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的开发人员来说，他们</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">的直觉可能会将他们引向灾难性的歧途。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">2.3.2</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">　语句并非按顺序执行</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 程序表现得仿佛它们是按顺序执行的，完全遵守了</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 流程控制语句的控制。上句话</span>
<span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">18   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">｜</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">第</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">2</span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章</span>

---

## Page 42

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">中的含糊其辞的“仿佛”正是许多编译器进行优化的基础，也是现代计算机硬件的许多技</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">巧的基础。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">当然，在底层，编译器能够而且有时也确实会对语句进行重新排序以改善性能。但是编译</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">器知道在测试一个变量或是将其赋值给另外一个变量之前，必须先确定它包含了所有的最</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">新计算结果。现代处理器也可能会选择乱序执行指令，不过它们包含了可以确保在随后读</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">取同一个内存地址之前，一定会先向该地址写入值的逻辑。甚至微处理器的内存控制逻辑</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">可能会选择延迟写入内存以优化内存总线的使用。但是内存控制器知道哪次写值正在从执</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">行单元穿越高速缓存飞往主内存的“航班”中，而且确保如果随后读取同一个地址时会使</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">用这个“航班”中的值。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">并发会让情况变得复杂。</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 程序在编译时不知道是否会有其他线程并发运行。</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C++</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 编译</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">器不知道哪个变量——如果有的话——会在线程间共享。当程序中包含共享数据的并发线</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">程时，编译器对语句的重排序和延迟写入主内存会导致计算结果与按顺序执行语句的计算</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">结果不同。开发人员必须向多线程程序中显式地加入同步代码来确保可预测的行为的一致</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">性。当并发线程共享数据时，同步代码降低了并发量。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">2.4</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">　小结</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">在处理器中，访问内存的性能开销远比其他操作的性能开销大。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">非对齐访问所需的时间是所有字节都在同一个字中时的两倍。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">访问频繁使用的内存地址的速度比访问非频繁使用的内存地址的速度快。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">访问相邻地址的内存的速度比访问互相远隔的地址的内存快。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">由于高速缓存的存在，一个函数运行于整个程序的上下文中时的执行速度可能比运行于</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">测试套件中时更慢。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">访问线程间共享的数据比访问非共享的数据要慢很多。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">计算比做决定快。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">每个程序都会与其他程序竞争计算机资源。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">如果一个程序必须在启动时执行或是在负载高峰期时执行，那么在测量性能时必须加载</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">负载。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">每一次赋值、函数参数的初始化和函数返回值都会调用一次构造函数，这个函数可能隐</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">藏了大量的未知代码。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">有些语句隐藏了大量的计算。从语句的外表上看不出语句的性能开销会有多大。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">当并发线程共享数据时，同步代码降低了并发量。</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">影响优化的计算机行为</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">｜</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   19</span>

---

## Page 43

<span style="font-family:'HYe3gj';font-size:19.00pt;color:#181818">第</span><span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:19.00pt;color:#181818">3</span><span style="font-family:'HYe3gj';font-size:19.00pt;color:#181818"> 章</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYb2gj';font-size:26.83pt;color:#181818">测量性能</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">测量可测量之物，将不可测量之物变为可测量。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">测量和实验是所有改善程序性能尝试的基础。本章将介绍两种测量性能的工具软件：分析</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">器和计时器软件。我将讨论如何设计性能测量实验，使得测量结果更有指导意义，而不是</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">误导我们。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">最基本和最频繁地执行的软件性能测量会告诉我们“需要多长时间”。执行函数需要多长</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">时间？从磁盘读取配置文件需要多长时间？启动和退出程序需要多长时间？</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">这些测量问题的解答方法有时简单得令人觉得可笑。牛顿通过用物体掉落至地面的时间除</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">以他的心跳速度测量出了重力常数</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:5.54pt;color:#181818">1</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">。我相信每位开发人员都有通过大声数数进行计时的经</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">历。在美国，我们通过喊“</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">one-Mississippi, two-Mississippi, three-Mississippi...</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">”</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:5.54pt;color:#181818">2</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">来得到比较</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">精确的秒数。带有秒表功能的电子手表曾经是计算机极客的必备之物，而非仅仅是潮流的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">象征。在嵌入式开发中，熟悉硬件的开发人员有很多优秀的工具可以使用，其中有频率计</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">数器和信号示波器等甚至可以精确地测量极短例程的时间的工具。软件厂商也会出售专业</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">工具，由于数量太多，这里不会逐一介绍。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">本章将主要介绍两种被广泛使用的、具有通用性且价格低廉的工具。第一个工具是编译器</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">厂商通常在编译器中都会提供的</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">分析器</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">proﬁler</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）。分析器会生成各个函数在程序运行过</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">程中被调用的累积时间的表格报表。对性能优化而言，它是一个非常关键的工具，因为它</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">注</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">1</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">：</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818"> </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">根据维基百科的记载牛顿只是提出了重力常数，重力常数是在</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">71</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818"> 年后通过扭秤实验</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">(</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818"> 卡文迪许实验</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">)</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">被测量出来的。——译者注。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">注</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">2</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">：</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818"> </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">很难找到这种计算秒数方法的起源，不过大部分人认为这是美国人在童年时就已经学会的一种数秒方</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">法，因为读完</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818">Mississippi</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:8.00pt;color:#181818"> 这个单词刚好大约需要一秒钟时间。——译者注</span>
<span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">20</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">——伽利略</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:7.00pt;color:#181818">•</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 伽利雷（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1564</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">—</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1642</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）</span>

![](./C++性能优化指南 (甘瑟尔罗斯) (Z-Library)_assets/images/p043_img01.png)

---

## Page 44

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">会列出程序中最热点的函数。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">第二个工具是</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">计时器软件</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">software timer</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）。开发人员可以自己实现这个工具，就像绝地武</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">士自己打造他们的光剑一样（请原谅我在这里引用了《星球大战》中的内容打比喻）。如</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">果带有分析器的豪华版编译器太过昂贵，或是编译器厂商在某些嵌入式平台上不提供分析</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">器，开发人员依然可以通过测量长时间运行的活动来进行性能实验。计时器软件还可以用</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">于测量不受计算限制的任务。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">第三个工具是非常古老的“实验笔记本”，许多开发人员认为它已经完全过时了。但是实</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">验笔记本或是其他文本文件仍然是不可或缺的优化工具。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">3.1</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">　优化思想</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">在开始介绍测量和实验之前，我想谈一点点我一直在实践的、也是我想在本书中教授的优</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">化哲学。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">3.1.1</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">　必须测量性能</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">人的感觉对于检测性能提高了多少来说是不够精确的。人的记忆力不足以准确地回忆起以</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">往多次实验的结果。书本中的知识可能会误导你，使你相信了一些并非总是正确的事情。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">当判断是否应当对某段代码进行优化的时候，开发人员的直觉往往差得令人吃惊。他们</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">编写了函数，也知道这个函数会被调用，但他们并不清楚调用频率以及会被什么代码所调</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">用。于是，一段低效的代码混入了核心组件中并被调用了无数次。经验也可能会欺骗你。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">编程语言、编译器、库和处理器都在不断地发展。之前曾经肯定是热点的函数可能会变得</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">非常高效，反之亦然。只有测量才能告诉你到底是在优化游戏中取胜了还是失败了。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">那些具有最让我折服的优化技巧的开发人员都会系统地完成他们的优化任务：</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">他们做出的预测都是可测试的，而且他们会记录下预测；</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">他们保留代码变更记录；</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">他们使用可以使用的最优秀的工具进行测量；</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">他们会保留实验结果的详细笔记。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">请回过头来再次阅读上节中的内容。其中包含了本书中最重要的建议。多数开发人员</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（包括笔者）都会想当然地，而不是按照以上方式有条不紊地进行优化。这是一项必须</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">不断实践的技能。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">3.1.2</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">　优化器是王牌猎人</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">我说起飞后用核弹炸掉这地方。这是唯一的方法。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">优化器是王牌猎人。如果只能让程序的运行速度提高</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1%</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 是不值得冒险去修改代码的，因</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:11.00pt;color:#181818">停下来思考</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">——艾伦</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:7.00pt;color:#181818">•</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 蕾普莉（西格丽</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:7.00pt;color:#181818">•</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 维弗饰演），《异形</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">2</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">》，</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1986</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 年</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">测量性能</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">｜</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   21</span>

---

## Page 45

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">为修改代码可能会引入</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">bug</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">。只有能显著地提升性能时才值得修改代码。而且，这</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1%</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">速度提升可能只是将测量套件的误差当作了性能改善。因此，我们必须用随机抽样统计</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">和置信水平来证明速度的提升。但是完全没有必要为了这么一点点性能提升花费这么大气</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">力。本书中不会推荐大家这么做。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">当性能提升</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">20%</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的时候，事情就完全不同了。它会消除所有反对方法论的声音。本书中虽</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">然没有太多统计数字，不过我并不会为此感到抱歉。本书的重点是帮助开发人员找到这样</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">的性能改善点：其显著的效果足以战胜任何对其价值的质疑。这些性能改善点可能仍然取</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">决于操作系统和编译器等因素，因此它们可能会在其他操作系统上或是其他时间点没有太</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">好的效果。但是即使开发人员把他们的代码移植到新操作系统上，这些修改也几乎从来都</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">不会反过来降低程序性能。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">3.1.3</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">　</span><span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">90/10</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">规则</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">性能优化的基本规则是</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">90/10</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 规则：一个程序花费</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">90%</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的时间执行其中</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10%</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的代码。这</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">只是一条启发性的规则，并非自然法则，但对于我们的思考和计划却具有指导性。这条规</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">则有时也被称为</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">80/20</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 规则，但思想是一样的。直观地说，</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">90/10</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 规则表示某些代码块是会</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">被频繁地执行的</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">热点</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">hot spot</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">），而其他代码则几乎不会被执行。这些热点就是我们要进</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">行性能优化的对象。</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:11.00pt;color:#181818">优化战争故事</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">我是在作为专业开发人员研发一种叫作</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">9010A</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的带键盘的嵌入式设备（图</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">3-1</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）的项</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">目中初识</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">90/10</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 规则的。</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYe3gj';font-size:9.01pt;color:#181818">图</span><span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:9.01pt;color:#181818">3-1</span><span style="font-family:'HYe3gj';font-size:9.01pt;color:#181818">：</span><span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:9.01pt;color:#181818">Fluke 9010A</span><span style="font-family:'HYe3gj';font-size:9.01pt;color:#181818">（英国计算机历史博物馆）</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">程序中有个函数会轮询键盘，查看用户是否按下了</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">STOP</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 键。这个函数会被每个例程</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">频繁地执行。手动优化</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 编译器输出的这个函数的</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Z80</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 汇编代码（耗费了</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">45</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 分钟）</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">将整体吞吐量提高了</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">7%</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">，对这台设备来说，非常不错了。</span>
<span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">22   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">｜</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">第</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">3</span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章</span>

![](./C++性能优化指南 (甘瑟尔罗斯) (Z-Library)_assets/images/p045_img01.jpg)

---

## Page 46

<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">一般情况下，这是一条典型的性能优化经验。在优化过程的初期，大量的运行时间都</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">集中消耗在程序中的某个位置。这个位置也非常明显：在每个循环的每次迭代中都要</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">重复进行的处理，就像每天的家务劳动一样。想要优化这些代码需要做出一项痛苦的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">选择——用汇编语言重写这些</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">C</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 语言代码。但是由于使用汇编语言的代码范围极其有</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">限，选择使用汇编语言降低了需要承受的风险。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">当这段代码被频繁执行时，这条经验同样很典型。当我们改善了这段代码后，另一段</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">代码成为了最频繁地被执行的代码——不过它对整体运行时间的影响已经小多了。它</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">实在是太小了，以至于我们在进行了这一处改动后就停止了性能优化。我们甚至找不</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">到改动后可以将程序执行速度提高</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1%</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的地方了。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">90/10</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 规则的一个结论是，优化程序中的所有例程并没有太大帮助。优化一小部分代码事</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">实上已经足够提供你所想要的性能提升了。识别出</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10%</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的热点代码是值得花费时间的，但</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">靠猜想选择优化哪些代码可能只是浪费时间。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">这里我想再一次引用第</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章中曾经引用过的高德纳的一句名言。不过，此处是那句名言一</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">个较长的版本：</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">其中</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">S</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:5.54pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">T</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 是因优化而导致程序整体性能提升的比率，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">P</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 是被优化部分的运行时间占原来程序</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">整体运行时间的比例，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">S</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:5.54pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">P</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 是被优化部分</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">P</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的性能改善的比率。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">例如，假设一个程序的运行时间是</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">100</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 秒。通过分析（请参见</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">3.3</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 节）发现程序花费了</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">80</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">秒多次调用函数</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">f</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">。现在假设修改</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">f</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 使其运行速度提升了</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">30%</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">，那么这对程序整体运行时</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">间有多大改善呢？</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">程序员浪费了太多的时间去思考和担忧程序中那些非关键部分的速度，而且考虑</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">到调试和维护，这些为优化而进行的修改实际上是有很大负面影响的。我们应当</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">忘记小的性能改善，</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">97%</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的情况下，过早优化都是万恶之源。</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">——高德纳，“使用</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">goto</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 语句进行结构化编程”，</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> ACM Computing Surveys 6  </span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">(Dec 1974): 268. CiteSeerX: 10.1.1.103.6084</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">http://citeseerx.ist.psu.edu/ </span>

<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">viewdoc/summary?doi=10.1.1.103.6084</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">正如有些人所建议的那样，高德纳博士也并非警告我们所有的优化都是罪恶的。他只是说</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">浪费时间去优化那非关键的</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">90%</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的程序是罪恶的。很明显，他也意识到了</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">90/10</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 规则。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">3.1.4</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">　阿姆达尔定律</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">阿姆达尔定律是由计算机工程先锋基恩</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:7.00pt;color:#181818">•</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 阿姆达尔（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Gene Amdahl</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）提出并用他的名字命名</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">的，它定义了优化一部分代码对整体性能有多大改善。阿姆达尔定律有多种表达方式，不</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">过就优化而言，可以表示为下面的等式：</span>

<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesItalic';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">S</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesItalic';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">P</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesItalic';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">S</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">=</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">-</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">+</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesItalic';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">P</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesItalic';font-size:6.00pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">T</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">(1</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">)</span>

<span style="font-family:'MMTimesItalic';font-size:6.00pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">P</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">测量性能</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">｜</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   23</span>

<span style="font-family:'MicrosoftYaHei';font-size:8.00pt;color:#b4b4b4">图灵社区会员 ChenyangGao(2339083510@qq.com) 专享 尊重版权</span>

## Page 47

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">P</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 是函数</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">f</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的运行时间占原来程序整体运行时间的比例，即</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">0.8</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">；</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">S</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:5.54pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">P</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 是被优化的部分</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">P</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">性能改善的比率，即</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1.3</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">。将它们代入到阿姆达尔定律的公式中：</span>

<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">0.2</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">0.62</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1.22</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesItalic';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">S</span><span style="font-family:'MMTimesItalic';font-size:6.00pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818"> T</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">-</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">+</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">=</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">+</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">=</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:12.00pt;color:#181818">=</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">(1</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">0.8)</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1.3</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">0.8</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">也就是说，将这个函数的性能提升</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">30%</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 会将程序整体运行时间缩短</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">22%</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">。在这个例子中，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">阿姆达尔定律证明了</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">90/10</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 规则，而且通过这个例子向我们展示了，对</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10%</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的热点代码进</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">行适当的优化，就可以带来如此大的性能提升。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">下面我们再来看一个例子。我们还是假设一个程序的运行时间是</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">100</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 秒。通过分析，你发</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">现有一个函数</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">g</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的运行时间是</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 秒。现在假设你修改了函数</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">g</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">，将它的运行速度提高了</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">100</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 倍。那么这对程序整体性能的提升有多大呢？</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">P</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 是函数</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">g</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的运行时间占原来程序整体运行时间的比例，即</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">0.1</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">；</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">S</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:5.54pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">P</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 是</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">100</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">。将它们代入到</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">阿姆达尔定律的公式中：</span>

<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 0.</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">0.</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1.</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesItalic';font-size:9.50pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818">S</span><span style="font-family:'MMTimesItalic';font-size:6.00pt;font-style:italic;color:#181818"> T</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">-</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">=</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">+</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">=</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">+</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">=</span>

<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">0.</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">9</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">001</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">11</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">(1</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">0. )</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1</span>
<span style="font-family:'MMTimesRoman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">00</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">在这个例子中阿姆达尔定律是具有警示性的。即使有异常优秀的编码能力或是黑科技将函</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">数</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">g</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的运行时间缩短为</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">0</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">，它仍然是那并不重要的</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">90%</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 代码中的一部分。将性能提升的比</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">率精确到两个小数位后，对程序整体性能的提升依然只有</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">11%</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">。阿姆达尔定律告诉我们，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">如果被优化的代码在程序整体运行时间中所占的比率不大，那么即使对它的优化非常成功</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">也是不值得的。阿姆达尔定律的教训是，当你的同事兴冲冲地在会议上说他知道如何将一</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">段计算处理的速度提高</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 倍，这并不一定意味着性能优化工作就此结束了。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">3.2</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:17.00pt;color:#181818">　进行实验</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">开发软件在某种意义上就是一项实验。你想让程序做一些事情，然后开始编程，最后观察</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">程序的运行结果是否与预想的一样。性能调优则是更有正式意义的实验。在开始性能调优</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">前，必须要有正确的代码，即在某种意义上可以完成我们所期待的处理的代码。你需要擦</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">亮眼睛审视这些代码，然后问自己：“为什么这些代码是热点？”为什么某个函数与程序</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">中的上百个函数不同，出现在了分析器的最差性能列表中的最前面？是这个函数浪费了很</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">多时间在冗余处理上吗？有其他更快的方法进行相同的计算吗？这个函数使用了紧缺的计</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">算机资源吗？是这个函数自身已经是非常快了，只不过它被调用了太多次，已经没有优化</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">的余地了吗？</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">你对于“为什么这些代码是热点”这个问题的回答构成了你要测试的假设。实验要对程序</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">的两种运行时间进行测量：一种是修改前的运行时间，一种是修改后的运行时间。如果后</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">者比前者短，那么实验验证了你的假设。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">请注意这里的用词。实验并不需要证明任何事情。修改后的代码可能会因为某些原因运行</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">得更快或者更慢，但这些原因却与你修改的部分没有任何关系。比如：</span>
<span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">24   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">｜</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">第</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">3</span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章</span>

---

## Page 48

<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">当你在测量运行时间时，计算机可能在接收邮件或是检查</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Java</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 是否有版本更新；</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">在你重编译之前，一位同事刚刚签入了一个性能改善后的库；</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">• </span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">你的修改可能运行得更快，但是处理逻辑却是不正确的。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">优秀的科学家是怀疑论者。他们总是对事物持有怀疑。如果没有出现所期待的实验结果，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">或是实验结果太好了，不像是对的，那么怀疑论者会再进行一次实验或者质疑她的假设，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">抑或检查是否有</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">bug</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">优秀的科学家会接受新知识，即使这些知识与他们脑海中的知识相悖。我在编写本书的过</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">程中学到了一些出乎意料的优化知识。本书的技术审核者也从本书中学到了知识。优秀的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">科学家从不会停止学习。</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:11.00pt;color:#181818">优化战争故事</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">在第</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">5</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章有一个查找关键字的示例函数。我为这个示例函数编写了几个不同的版本。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">其中一个版本是</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">线性查找</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">linear search</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">），另一个版本则是</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">二分查找</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">binary search</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">当测量这两个函数的性能时，我发现线性查找的速度比二分查找快几个百分点。这让</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">我觉得不可思议。二分查找本应当更快，但是测量结果却不是这样的。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">我注意到有人在互联网上发表报告说线性查找经常会更快，因为相比二分查找，它的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">缓存局部性</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">cache locality</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）更好，而且确实我实现的线性查找应当具有非常优秀的缓</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">存局部性。但是这个结果却与我的经验以及我从受人尊崇的书本上学到的有关查找算</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">法性能的知识相违背。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">进行了更深入的调查后我发现，在测试时所使用的测试表格中只有几个单词，而且要</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">查找的关键字我自己都能从表格中找到。如果一个表格有</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">8</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 个项目，那么线性查找平</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">均会检查其中半数（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">4</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）后返回结果。而二分查找每次被调用时都会将表格一分为二</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">（共</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">4</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 次），然后才能查找到关键字。这两种算法对小的关键字集有着完全相同的平均</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">性能。直觉告诉我二分查找总是比线性查找更快，但这个结果告诉我我错了。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">但是这并非我想证明的结果。所以我扩大了测试数据表格，想着这个表格在达到某</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">个大小时，一定会出现二分查找更快的结果。另外，我还向其中加入了一些原本不</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">在测试表格中的单词。可是测试结果依然不变，线性查找更快。这时，我不得不将</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">编写这份示例代码的任务搁置了几天，但是这个结果却一直折磨着我。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">我仍然相信二分查找应当更快。我检查了两种查找方式的单元测试代码，最终发现线</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">性查找在进行第一次比较后总是返回成功。我的测试用例检查了是否返回了非零值，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">而不是检查是否返回了正确值。接着，我惭愧地修改了线性查找算法和测试用例。现</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">在，实验结果与我所期待的一样，二分查找的速度更快了。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">在这个例子中，实验结果先否定然后又验证了我的假设——整个过程中一直在挑战</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">我的假设。</span>

<span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">测量性能</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">｜</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   25</span>

---

## Page 49

<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">3.2.1</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">　记实验笔记</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">优秀的优化人员（如同所有优秀的科学家）都会关心可重复性。这时实验室笔记本就可以</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">发挥作用了。为了验证猜想，优化人员在对代码进行一处或多处修改后，利用输入数据集</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">对代码进行性能测试，而测试则会在若干毫秒后结束。在与下次运行时间进行比较前一直</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">记着上次程序的运行时间，这事儿并不难。如果每次代码改善都是成功的，用脑袋记住就</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">足够了。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">不过，开发人员的猜想可能会出错，这将导致最近一次的程序运行时间比上一次的更长。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">这时，无数的疑问会充斥在开发人员的脑中。虽然</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">5</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 号测试的运行时间比</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">4</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 号长，但是它</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">比</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">3</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 号短吗？在进行</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">3</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 号测试时修改了哪些代码？两次测试间的速度差异是由其他因素造</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">成的，还是的确变快了？</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">如果每次的测试运行情况都被记录在案，那么就可以快速地重复实验，回答上述问题就会</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">变得很轻松了。否则，开发人员必须回过头去重新做一次实验来获取运行时间——前提是</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">他还记得应该修改哪些代码或是撤销哪些修改。如果测试运行很简单，开发人员的记忆力</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">也非常好，那么他很幸运，只需要花费一点时间即可重复实验。但是也有可能没那么幸</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">运，明明想重复实验却偏离了正确的前进道路，或是毫无意义地浪费一天去重复实验。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">每当我给出这条建议时，总会有人说：“我不需要笔和纸就能做到！我可以写一段</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Perl</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 脚</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">本去修改代码版本管理工具的命令，让它帮忙将每次运行的测试结果和所修改的代码一起</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">保存起来。如果我将测试结果保存在文件中……如果我在不同的目录下做测试……”</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">我并不想妨碍开发人员创新。如果你是一位主动吸收最佳实践的高级开发经理，那么尽管</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">这么做吧。不过我想说的是，使用纸和笔记录是一种很稳健、容易使用而且有着千年历史</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">的技术。即使在开发团队替换了版本管理工具或测试套件的情况下，这项技术仍然可用。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">它还适用于开发人员的下一份工作。这项传统的解决方案仍然可以节省开发人员的时间。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">3.2.2</span><span style="font-family:'HYb1gj';font-size:14.00pt;color:#181818">　测量基准性能并设定目标</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">独立开发人员可以随意地、迭代地进行优化，直到他觉得性能足够好了为止。不过工作于</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">团队中的开发人员需要满足经理和其他利益相关人员的需求。优化工作受两个数字主导：</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">优化前的性能基准测量值和性能目标值。测量性能基准不仅对于衡量每次独立的改善是否</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">成功非常重要，而且对于向其他利益相关人员就优化成本开销做出解释也是非常重要的。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">而优化目标值之所以重要，是因为在优化过程中优化效果会逐渐变小。在优化过程的最初</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">阶段，树上总是有些容易摘取的挂得很低的水果：一些独立的进程或是想当然地编写的函</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">数，优化它们后可以使性能提升很多。但是一旦实现了这些简单的优化目标后，下一轮性</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">能提升就需要付出更多的努力。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">许多团队之所以在一开始没有为性能或是响应性设定目标，只是因为他们并不习惯这么</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">做。幸运的是，差劲的性能往往表现得非常明显（例如用户界面长时间不响应、托管服</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">务器的规模没有可扩展性、按照</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 时间付费的成本非常高等）。一旦团队研究下性能问</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">题，那么目标数字很容易被设定下来。用户体验（</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">UX</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">）设计的一个学科分支专门研究用</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">户如何看待等待时间。下面是一份常用的性能测试项目清单，你可以从为这些项目设定性</span>
<span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">26   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">｜</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">第</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">3</span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 章</span>

---

## Page 50

<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">能目标开始。这其中有足够多的与用户体验相关的数字，可以让你意识到危险性。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">启动时间</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">从用户按下回车键直至程序进入主输入处理循环所经过的时间。通常，开发人员可以通</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">过测量程序进入</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">main()</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 函数到进入主循环的时间来得到启动时间，但是有时候也有例</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">外。为程序提供认证的操作系统厂商对程序在计算机启动时或某个用户登入时就运行有</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">严格的要求。例如，对那些寻求认证的硬件厂商，微软会要求</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">Windows shell</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 必须在启</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">动后</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 秒内能够进入它们的主循环。这限制了在忙碌的启动环境中，厂商可以预载和</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">启动的其他程序的数量。为此，微软提供了专用工具来帮助硬件厂商测量启动时间。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">退出时间</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">从用户点击关闭图标或是输入退出命令直至程序实际完全退出所经过的时间。通常，开</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">发人员可以通过测量主窗口接收到关闭命令到程序退出</span><span style="font-family:'UbuntuMono-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#181818">main()</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的时间来得到退出时间，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">但是有时候也有例外。退出时间也包含停止所有的线程和所依赖的进程所需的时间。为</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">程序提供认证的操作系统厂商对程序的退出时间有严格的要求。退出时间同样非常重</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">要，因为重启一个服务或是长时间运行的程序所需的时间等于它的退出时间加上它的启</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">动时间。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">响应时间</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">执行一个命令的平均时间或最长时间。对于网站来说，平均响应时间和最长响应时间</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">都会影响用户对网站的满意度。响应时间可以粗略地以</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 的幂为单位划分为以下几</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">个级别。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">低于</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">0.1</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 秒：用户在直接控制</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">如果响应时间低于</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">0.1</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 秒，用户会感觉他们在直接控制用户界面，他们的操作直接</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">改变了用户界面。这是用户开始拖动对象至对象发生移动，或是用户点击输入框至</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">输入框变为高亮之间的最小延迟。任何高于这个值的延迟都会让用户觉得他们发送</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">了一条命令让计算机去执行。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">0.1</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 秒至</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 秒：用户在控制命令</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">如果响应时间在</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">0.1</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 秒至</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 秒之间，用户虽然仍然会觉得他们处于掌控状态，但是</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">这个短暂的延迟会被用户理解为计算机执行了一条命令导致</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">UI</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 发生了变化。用户可</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">以忍受这种程度的延迟，不至于分散注意力。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 秒至</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 秒：计算机在控制</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">如果响应时间在</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">1</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 秒至</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 秒之间，用户会觉得他们在执行了一条命令后失去了对</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">计算机的控制，虽然这时候计算机仍然在处理命令。用户可能会分散注意力，忘记</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">一件刚才发生的事情——他们需要完成自己的任务。</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 秒是用户能保持注意力的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">最长时间。如果他们多次遇到这种长时间等待</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">UI</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 发生改变的情况，用户满意度会</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">急速下降。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">高于</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10</span><span style="font-family:'HYc1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 秒：喝杯咖啡休息一下</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">如果响应时间高于</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">10</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818"> 秒，用户会觉得他们有足够的时间去做一些其他的事情。如</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">果他们的工作需要用到</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">UI</span><span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">，那么他们会利用等待计算机进行计算的时间去喝一杯</span>
<span style="font-family:'HYa1gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">咖啡。如果可以的话，他们甚至会关闭程序，然后去其他地方找找满足感。</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">  </span>

<span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">测量性能</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   </span><span style="font-family:'HYg2gj';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">｜</span><span style="font-family:'MyriadPro-Regular';font-size:9.50pt;color:#181818">   27</span>
